
-----title

gray;'>▪</span>在润州，润州司马任上。许浑重游练湖怀旧，有诗一首。作品：《重游练湖怀旧》《秋晚云阳驿西亭莲池》<div id='poem_20224' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20224' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20224?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20159'>烟开翠扇清风晓，水泥<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作泛）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_20159", 20159, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>红衣</span>白露秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20159'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1414, "poem_sentence_2_20159")'>神女</span>暂来云易散，仙娥初<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作终）</span>去月难留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20159'>空怀远道难<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作无）</span>持赠，醉倚阑干<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作西阑）</span>尽日愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20159_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=827&endYear=827')">827年</a>　大和元年，许浑再试下第。别好友杨发，有诗。作品：《下第别杨至之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（杨发，字至之，先为同州冯翊人，父遗直始家于苏州。生卒年均不详，约唐武宗会昌中前后在世。工于诗。太和四年，（公元八三o年）登进士第。历太常少卿，出为苏州刺史。后为岭南节度，严于治军。军人遂怨起为乱，囚发于邮舍。坐贬婺州刺史，卒于任。发为诗清新浏亮，传世颇多。唐代著名诗人。（百度百科））</span><div id='poem_19965' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　许浑返长安。闻宋申锡谪死开州，作诗伤之。作品：《闻开江相国宋公下世二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋申锡（公元760年－834年8月13日[1] ）[2] ，字庆臣，今湖南省汝城县泉水乡石塘（唐朝时原义昌县府驻地）人。生于公元760年。宝历三年826年任礼部员外郎，828年进中书舍人，翰林学士，830年任同中书门下平章事（宰相），834年卒于开州贬所，836年诏追复尚书右丞、同中书门下平章事，赠兵部尚书，谥曰文懿。在唐文宗年间短暂担任宰相。他意图帮助文宗清除权阉，反被诬指企图推翻文宗改立其皇弟（漳王李凑）而遭贬死。（百度百科））</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb8d0e11a88e4927aa25fc8eb63be04e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb8d0e11a88e4927aa25fc8eb63be04e");'><span id='bb8d0e11a88e4927aa25fc8eb63be04e_link' -----title
三门峡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e752e429a9124800a8cccbc2d301e999_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e752e429a9124800a8cccbc2d301e999");'><span id='e752e429a9124800a8cccbc2d301e999_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>，20岁</div><div id='e752e429a9124800a8cccbc2d301e999' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑初赴京参加进士试，过陕州。夜宴将罢，作诗一首。作品：《听歌鹧鸪词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此条活动具体时间不详，但确定在公元807-810之间，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_20051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>听歌鹧鸪辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20051")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20051_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_20051'>余过陕州，夜宴将罢，妓人善歌鹧鸪者，词调清怨，往往在耳，因题是诗。</div><div id='poem_preface_20051_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20051'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(61, "poem_allusion_20051")'>甘棠</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20051'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20051'>南国多情多艳词，鹧鸪清怨绕梁飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20051'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(61, "poem_sentence_1_20051")'>甘棠</span>城上客先醉，苦竹岭头人未归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20051'>响转碧霄云驻影，曲终清漏月沈晖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20051'>山行水宿不知远，犹梦玉钗金缕衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20051'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20051_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑初赴京参加进士试，与友人张厚同行，至陕州，二人作别，作诗一首别送张厚。作品：《别张秀才》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此条活动具体时间不详，但确定在公元807-810之间，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_20049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别张秀才</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20049")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20049_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_20049'>余与张秀才同出关至陕府，余取南道止洛下（余取南道至洛下），张由北路抵江东，因幕中宴饯，遂赋诗以别。</div><div id='poem_preface_20049_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20049'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(771, "poem_allusion_20049")'>人生贵适意</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20049'>不知何计写离忧，万里山川半旧游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20049'>风捲暮沙和雪起，日融春水带冰流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20049'>凌晨客泪分东郭，竟夕乡心共北楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20049'>青桂一枝年少<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作少年）</span>事，莫因鲈鲙涉穷秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20049'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20049_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜阳（寿安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='40e20ef36a38414c98c35cab49f92827_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("40e20ef36a38414c98c35cab49f92827");'><span id='40e20ef36a38414c98c35cab49f92827_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>，20岁</div><div id='40e20ef36a38414c98c35cab49f92827' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　许浑欲进京干禄，早发寿安济永济渡口，有诗一首。作品：《早发寿安济永济渡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷三，此条活动具体时间不详，但据诗意确定为早年移家巩洛时进京干禄所作。）</span><div id='poem_20022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>早发寿安次永寿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作济）</span>渡</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20022")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20022'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20022'>东西车马尘，巩洛与咸秦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20022'>山月夜行客，水烟朝渡人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20022'>树凉风<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_20022", 20022, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>皓皓</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作浩浩）</span>，滩浅石磷磷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20022'>会待功名就，扁舟寄此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20022'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20022_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d19101f4b32d42d1b3f49132eb39c046_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d19101f4b32d42d1b3f49132eb39c046");'><span id='d19101f4b32d42d1b3f49132eb39c046_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>，23岁</div><div id='d19101f4b32d42d1b3f49132eb39c046' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑因落第，在颍州幕府从事。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑在颍州幕府从事。作诗送郭秀才。作品：《送郭秀才游天台》<div id='poem_20208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送郭秀才游天台</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20208")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20208_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_20208'>余尝与郭秀才同玩朱审画天台山图，秀才因游是山，题诗赠别。</div><div id='poem_preface_20208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20208'>云埋阴壑雪凝峰，半壁天台已万重。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20208'>人度碧溪疑辍棹，僧归苍岭似闻钟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20208'>暖眠鸂鶒晴滩<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作天）</span>草，高挂猕猴暮涧松。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20208'>曾约共<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作旧）</span>游今独去，赤城西面<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作香炉山下）</span>水溶溶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20208'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在颍州，从事西湖亭宴饯，许浑作诗一首，姑系于此。作品：《颍州从事西湖亭宴饯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_20311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍州从事西湖亭宴饯</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20311")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20311'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20311'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_20311", 20311, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>西湖</span>清宴不知回，一曲离歌酒一杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20311'>城带夕阳闻鼓角，寺临秋水见楼台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20311'>兰堂客散<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作醉）</span>蝉犹噪，桂楫人稀鸟自来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20311'>独想征车过<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作帆去）</span>巩洛，此中霜菊绕潭<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作正花）</span>开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20311'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，许浑奉使赴上都，僚吏于西湖中宴饯送行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5c99102499ac4e52af5df523d9099c56_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5c99102499ac4e52af5df523d9099c56");'><span id='5c99102499ac4e52af5df523d9099c56_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>，24岁</div><div id='5c99102499ac4e52af5df523d9099c56' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在颍州，友人李诩来访，许浑有诗相赠。作品：《喜李诩秀才见访因赠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷五，但诗题中“李翊”疑为“李诩”。此诗具体时间地点不详，但大致确定作于元和五、六年，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_20296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜李诩秀才见访因赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20296")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20296'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20296'>浙南分首日，谁谓别经时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20296'>路远遥相访，家贫喜见知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20296'>不须辞小酌，更请续新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20296'>但得心中剑，酬恩会有期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20296'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20296_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
洛阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=852&endYear=852')">852年</a>　八月中秋前分司东都，许浑赴洛阳。作品：《玩残雪寄河南刘大夫》<div id='poem_20095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_20095_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=853&endYear=853')">853年</a>　在洛阳。许浑以虞部员外郎分司东都，与河南尹刘瑑过从甚密。有诗赠刘瑑。作品：《分司东都寓居履道叨承三川守刘侍郎大夫恩知上四十韵》《早秋寄刘尚书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷九。）</span>《中秋日拜起居表晨渡天津桥即事十六韵献居守相国崔公兼呈工部刘公》《中秋夕寄大梁刘尚书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘瑑者，彭城人。祖璠，父煟。瑑，开成初进士擢第。会昌末，累迁尚书郎、知制诰，正拜中书舍人。大中初，转刑部侍郎。瑑精于法律，选大中以前二百四十四年制敕可行用者二千八百六十五条，分为六百四十六门，议其轻重，别成一家法书，号《大中统类》，奏行用之。出为河南尹，迁检校工部尚书、汴州刺史、宣武军节度使。十一年五月，加检校礼部尚书、太原尹、北都留守、河东节度观察等使。其年十二月入朝，拜户部侍郎，判度支。寻以本官同平章事，领使如故。十二年，累加集贤殿大学士。罢相，又历方镇，卒。事见《旧唐书·刘瑑传》（见《丁卯集笺证》卷九，第265页））</span><div color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑再游越中。有诗一首。作品：《山行至双岩溪访元隐居已榜舟诣开元寺水阁见送棹回已暮因赠》（犬吠双岩碧树间）<div id='poem_20043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_20043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20043'>栎坞炭烟晴过岭，蓼村渔火<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作父）</span>夜移湾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20043'>故乡芜没兵戈后，凭向溪南买一山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abe0cb0b293a4d5da782b87326fe175f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abe0cb0b293a4d5da782b87326fe175f");'><span id='abe0cb0b293a4d5da782b87326fe175f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年</a>，25岁</div><div id='abe0cb0b293a4d5da782b87326fe175f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='83215f48cf014f1885608aaba0e0ce65_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("83215f48cf014f1885608aaba0e0ce65");'><span id='83215f48cf014f1885608aaba0e0ce65_link' -----title
江陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='57d84c3517b14d9f8683a1ee0d13553c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("57d84c3517b14d9f8683a1ee0d13553c");'><span id='57d84c3517b14d9f8683a1ee0d13553c_link' 九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='503bf336e2dc4c97ab8583698907e335_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("503bf336e2dc4c97ab8583698907e335");'><span id='503bf336e2dc4c97ab8583698907e335_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>，32岁</div><div id='503bf336e2dc4c97ab8583698907e335' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f6f8d40062724e50af8f6664b6c14771_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f6f8d40062724e50af8f6664b6c14771");'><span id='f6f8d40062724e50af8f6664b6c14771_link' class='inlineComment2'>（王播（759～830）字明敭（同“扬”），太原（今太原）人。贞元（786～805年）中擢进士，举贤良方正异等。长庆初历进中书侍郎同中书门下平章事。太和初拜左仆射，封太原郡公。卒，谥曰敬。工书，尝书唐凤翔尹李晟为国修寺碑。《唐书本传》、《墨池编》、《佩文斋书画谱》。（见百度百科））</span><div id='poem_20081' -----title
河津（龙门）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3cb0585dda974f94a86b71664247b320_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3cb0585dda974f94a86b71664247b320");'><span id='3cb0585dda974f94a86b71664247b320_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>，37岁</div><div id='3cb0585dda974f94a86b71664247b320' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　长庆四年，许浑北游塞上，经龙门，晚登龙门驿楼，有诗一首。作品：《晚登龙门驿楼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_20286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚登龙门驿楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20286")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20286_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20286'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6752, "poem_allusion_20286")'>暴泥</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20286'>鱼龙多处凿门开，万古人知夏禹材。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20286'>青嶂远分从地断，洪流高泻自天来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20286'>风云有路皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_20286", 20286, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>烧尾</span>，波浪无程尽曝腮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20286'>心感膺门身过此，晚山秋树独徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20286'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20286_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
榆林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2710f6b6be69451d86492e1c4be48b2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2710f6b6be69451d86492e1c4be48b2f");'><span id='2710f6b6be69451d86492e1c4be48b2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>，37岁</div><div id='2710f6b6be69451d86492e1c4be48b2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　许浑塞上之行，是年秋，过榆林。有诗赠杜牧。作品：《孤雁》<div id='poem_20089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孤雁</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20089")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20089'>昔年双<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_20089", 20089, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>颉颃</span>，池上霭春晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20089'>霄汉力犹怯，稻粱心已违。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20089'>芦洲寒独宿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作立）</span>，榆塞夜孤飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20089'>不及营巢燕，西风相伴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作逐）</span>归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20089'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20089_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
蓟县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='be7b14d46093433aa26fd0f85534ded2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be7b14d46093433aa26fd0f85534ded2");'><span id='be7b14d46093433aa26fd0f85534ded2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>，38岁</div><div id='be7b14d46093433aa26fd0f85534ded2' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，许浑抵蓟州。幽州军乱，恶节度使藩镇拥兵自重，旋返。杜牧有诗答许浑所赠诗《孤雁》<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，许浑抵蓟州。幽州军乱，恶节度使藩镇拥兵自重，旋返。有诗寄刘三复。作品：《春日思旧游寄南徐从事刘三复》<div id='poem_20135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春日思旧游寄南徐从事刘三复</a><span class='authorDate'>（825年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20135")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20135_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20135'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2660, "poem_allusion_20135")'>燕台</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20135'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20135'>风暖曲江花半开，忽思京口共衔杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20135'>湘潭云尽暮山出，巴蜀雪消春水来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20135'>怀玉尚悲迷楚塞，捧金犹羡乐<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2660, "poem_sentence_2_20135")'>燕台</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20135'>蓟门高处极归思，陇雁北飞双燕回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20135_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
永济
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6b56051de81b479fbb16b1a8a1825c12_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b56051de81b479fbb16b1a8a1825c12");'><span id='6b56051de81b479fbb16b1a8a1825c12_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=826&endYear=826')">826年</a>，39岁</div><div id='6b56051de81b479fbb16b1a8a1825c12' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
长治

-----title
山西

-----title
晋城

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=841')">841年</a>　许浑在太平令任上，回润州，访浙西观察使卢简辞，有诗相和。作品：《奉和卢大夫新立假山诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（卢简辞父卢纶，著名诗人。卢简辞与兄卢简能，弟卢弘止、卢简求都中士，有文名。卢简辞初仕，三任地方节度使幕僚，长庆末(824年)入朝为监察御史，后升任侍御史，卢简辞当时对福建地区管理盐铁官卢昴的贪污案穷追不放，共查得赃钱30万缗，并从其家中搜出金床，及斗大的瑟瑟枕等，对这些赃物，唐敬宗都感叹没有见过。侍御史任后，卢简辞被太原节度使李程表求为判官，之后又入朝先后任考功员外郎，考功郎中、太仆卿等职。唐文宗大和年间 (827—835年)，他因事被贬为衢州刺史，唐武宗会昌年间(841—846年)被召入朝，先后任刑部侍郎、户部侍郎等职，唐宣宗大中元年(847年)迁兵部侍郎，兼工部尚书、许州刺史，御史大夫、忠武军节度使等多种职务。此后，他还任过湖南、浙西观察使，山南东道节度使等职。后卒于任上。卢简辞学识渊博，任侍御史时，严于执法，勇于断决，颇有一番作为。后主要历地方观察使、节座使等职。唐后期地方长吏专权一方，多横生事端。卢简辞虽政绩不显，但史书无载其为非之事，也颇为难得。（百度百科））</span><div id='poem_20390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和卢大夫新立假山</a><span class='authorDate'>（841年）</span><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=846&endYear=846')">846年8月</a>　在润州，润州司马任上。八月，许浑闻李珏由昭州刺史移郴州刺史，作诗寄李珏。作品：《闻韶州李相公移拜郴州因寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（李珏，字待价，其先出赵郡，客居淮阴。开成中，杨嗣复得君，引珏同中书门下平章事，与李固言皆善。后迁门下侍郎，为文宗山陵使。又贬江西观察使，再贬昭州刺史。宣宗立，内徙郴、舒二州，以太子宾客分司东都。迁河阳节度使。俄检校尚书右仆射、淮南节度使。珏顾己大臣，谊不以内外自异，表请立皇太子维天下心。江淮旱，发仓廪赈流民，以军羡储杀半价与人。卒，年六十九，赠司空，谥曰贞穆。（百度百科））</span><div -----title
吉安（庐陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='470d7377bf8448fd8d73a71942b94e64_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("470d7377bf8448fd8d73a71942b94e64");'><span id='470d7377bf8448fd8d73a71942b94e64_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>，49岁</div><div id='470d7377bf8448fd8d73a71942b94e64' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑行至庐陵，逢表兄军倅奉使淮海。作品：《别表兄军倅》<div id='poem_20050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别表兄军倅</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20050")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20050_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_20050'>余祗命南海，至庐陵，逢表兄军倅奉使淮海，别后却寄是诗。</div><div id='poem_preface_20050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20050'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20050'>卢橘花香拂钓矶，佳人犹舞越罗衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20050'>三洲水浅鱼来少，五岭山高雁到稀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20050'>客路晚依红树宿，乡关朝<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作晴，一作暗）</span>望白云归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20050'>交亲不念征南吏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作史，一作客）</span>，昨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作一）</span>夜风帆去似飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20050'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20050_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑过庐陵。有诗寄吉州刺史滕迈。作品：《舟行早发庐陵郡郭寄滕郎中》<div id='poem_20037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舟行早发庐陵郡郭寄滕郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20037")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20037_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20037'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(853, "poem_allusion_20037")'>相如渴</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1451, "poem_allusion_20037")'>曼倩</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20037'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20037'>楚客停桡太守知，露凝丹叶自秋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作愁）</span>悲<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20037'>蟹螯只恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(853, "poem_sentence_1_20037")'>相如渴</span>，鲈鲙应防<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作方）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1451, "poem_sentence_1_20037")'>曼倩</span>饥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20037'>风捲曙云飘角远，雨昏寒浪挂帆迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20037'>离心更羡高斋夕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作梦）</span>，巫峡花深醉玉卮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20037'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20037_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

韶关

-----title
清远
-----detail

href='/Writing/20384?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（837年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_20384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20384'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20384'>密树分苍壁，长溪抱碧岑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20384'>海<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作山）</span>风闻鹤远，潭日见鱼深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20384'>松盖环清韵，榕根架绿阴<span class='inlineComment2'>（南方有大叶榕树，枝垂入地生根）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20384'>洞丁多<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_20384", 20384, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>斲石</span>，蛮女<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作客）</span>半淘金<span class='inlineComment2'>（端州斲石，涂涯县淘金为业）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20384'>南浦惊春至，西楼送月沈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_20384'>江流不过岭，何处寄归心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_20384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_20384'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_20384_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_20385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20385?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_20385'>月在行人起，千峰复万峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20385'>海虚争翡翠，溪逻斗芙蓉<sup class='reference class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20385'>火探深洞燕，香送远潭龙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20385'>蓝坞寒先烧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_20385", 20385, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>禾堂</span>晚并舂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_20385'>更投何处宿，西峡隔云钟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_20385'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_20385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_20385'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_20385_0'>⑴ 南方呼市为虚，呼戍为逻，新州有翡翠虚、芙蓉逻</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_20385_0'>⑵ 木槲花生于他树槎蘖，池沼多松，谓之水松</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_20385_0'>⑶ 南方持火于乳洞中，取燕而食。康州悦城县，有温媪龙，即蛇也，随水往舟船至人家，或千里外，皆以香酒果送之</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_20385_0'>⑷ 种蓝多在坞中，先烧其地，人以木槽舂禾，谓之禾堂</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_20385_comment'></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_20385'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(20385)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>

当涂

id='poem_sentence_4_20223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=838&endYear=838')">838年</a>　在当涂，当涂尉任上。许浑有诗咏郁林寺。作品：《郁林寺》<div id='poem_20102' id='poem_title_20126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20126'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20126'>草堂近西郭，遥对敬<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作镜）</span>亭开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20126'>枕腻海<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作江）</span>云起，簟凉山雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20126'>高歌怀地肺，远赋忆天台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑再游越中。与台州刺史郑薰交游甚厚，有诗赠之。作品：《陪越中使院诸公镜波馆饯明台裴郑二使君》<span class='inlineComment2'>（生卒年不详。字子溥。文宗大和二年(828)登进士第，任户部员外郎、郎中。武宗会昌六年(846)，任台州刺史，转漳州刺史，入为考功郎中。宣宗大中三年(849)，充翰林学士、加知制诰。后拜中书舍人，工、礼二部侍郎。十年，自河南尹改宣歙观察使。性廉正，将吏不喜，共谋逐之，薰遂奔之扬州。贬棣王府长史，分司东都。懿宗立，召为太常少卿，累擢吏部侍郎。后以太子少师致仕，号“七松处士”。生平详见《唐阙史》卷上、《新唐书》本传、《唐诗纪事》卷五〇、《嘉定赤城志》卷八。薰能诗善文。《全唐诗》存诗1首，《全唐诗外编》补诗1首。（百度百科））</span><div id='poem_20263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪越中使院诸公镜波馆饯明台裴郑二使君</a><span class='authorDate'>（845年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20263")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20263'>倾幕来华馆，淹留二使君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20263'>舞移清夜月，歌断碧空云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20263'>海郡楼台接，江船剑戟分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20263'>明时自骞翥，无复叹离群。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20263'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20263_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>许浑再游越中。与台州刺史郑薰交游甚厚，陪郑薰泛舟，有诗一首。作品：《陪郑使君泛舟晚归》<div id='poem_20260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪郑史君泛舟晚归</a><span class='authorDate'>（845年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20260")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20260_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20260'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9652, "poem_allusion_20260")'>羊公</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20260'>南郭望归处，郡楼高卷帘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20260'>平桥低皂盖，曲岸转彤襜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20260'>江晚笙歌促，山晴鼓角严。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20260'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9652, "poem_sentence_3_20260")'>羊公</span>莫先醉，清晓月纤纤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20260'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20260_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
潼关
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3157ab488de043299d3539d955076593_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3157ab488de043299d3539d955076593");'><span id='3157ab488de043299d3539d955076593_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=848&endYear=848')">848年</a>，61岁</div><div id='3157ab488de043299d3539d955076593' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
建德

-----title
京山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='918e882a56bb4f7aad95aad08f49d9ed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("918e882a56bb4f7aad95aad08f49d9ed");'><span id='918e882a56bb4f7aad95aad08f49d9ed_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=854&endYear=854')">854年4月</a>　春深，赴任郢州刺史，许浑有诗和友人。作品：《酬钱汝州诗》<div id='poem_20322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>詶钱汝州</a><span class='authorDate'>（854年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20322")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20322_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_20322'>汝州钱中丞以浑赴郢城（汝州钱中丞以浑赴郢几），见寄佳什，恩怜过等，宠饰逾深，虽吟咏忘疲，实楷模不及，辄率荒浅，依韵献酬。</div><div id='poem_preface_20322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20322'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20322'>白雪多随汉水流，谩劳旌旆晚悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20322'>笙歌暗写终年恨，台榭潜消尽日忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20322'>鸟散落花人自醉，马嘶芳草客先愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20322'>怪来雅韵清无敌，三十六峰当庾楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20322'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=854&endYear=854')">854年</a>　在郢州，郢州刺史任上。李群之过郡，许浑宴饯之，有诗一首。作品：《宴饯李员外》<div id='poem_20237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宴饯李员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（854年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_20237'>李群之员外从事荆南尚书阳公，诏徵赴阙，俄为淮南相国杜公辟命，自汉上舟行至此郡，于云楼宴罢解缆，阻风却回，因赠。</div><div id='poem_preface_20237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20237'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20237'>病守江城眼暂开，昔年吴越共衔杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20237'>膺舟出镇虚陈榻，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_20237'>云叶渐低<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_20237", 20237, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>朱阁</span>掩，浪花初起<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_20237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=854&endYear=854')">854年8月</a>　在郢州，郢州刺史任上。秋八月，汉水伤稼，许浑有诗记之。作品：《汉水伤稼》<div id='poem_20004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉水伤稼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作杜牧诗）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_20291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20291'>山翠万重当槛出，水华千里抱城来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20291'>东岩月在僧初定<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作起）</span>，南浦花残客未<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作已）</span>回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20291'>欲吊灵均能赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作去）</span>否，秋风还有木兰开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20291'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20291_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=857&endYear=857')">857年</a>　在郢州，郢州刺史任上。许浑病间作诗寄郡中文士。作品：《病间寄郡中文士》<div id='poem_20253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病间寄郡中文士</a><span class='authorDate'>（857年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20253")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20253'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20253'>卢橘含花处处香，老人依旧卧清漳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20253'>心同客舍惊秋早，迹似僧斋厌夜长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20253'>风捲翠帘琴自响，露凝朱阁簟先凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20253'>明朝欲醉文中彦，犹觉吟声带越乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20253'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=857&endYear=857')">857年</a>　在郢州，郢州刺史任上。许浑病间作诗感怀。作品：《病中二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《丁卯集笺证》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_20251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（857年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19980, "唐", "许浑", "poem_title_20251")'>许浑</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20251_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_20251'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1511, "poem_allusion_20251")'>挂冠</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4416, "poem_allusion_20251")'>扃门卧</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_20251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20251'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20251'>三年婴酒渴，高卧似袁安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20251'>秋色鬓应改，夜凉心已宽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20251'>风衣藤簟滑，露井竹床寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20251'>卧忆郊扉月，恩深未<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1511, "poem_sentence_3_20251")'>挂冠</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20251'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20251_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_20252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_20252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/20252?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（857年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_20252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_20252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_20252'>私<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作欲）</span>归人暂适<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作静）</span>，扶杖绕西林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_20252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_20252'>风急柳溪响，露寒莎径深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_20252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_20252'>一身仍白发，万虑只丹心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_20252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_20252'>此意无言处，高窗托素琴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_20252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_20252'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_20252_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
